<span class="akn-akomaNtoso"><article class="akn-act" data-contains="originalVersion" data-name="act"><section class="akn-preface" id="preface"><span class="akn-p">Under section 156 of the <a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1996/constitution" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1996/constitution">Constitution of the Republic of South Africa, 1996</a>, the Bergrivier Municipality, enacts as follows:—</span></section><span class="akn-body"><section class="akn-section" id="sec_1" data-eId="sec_1"><h3>1. Definitions</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">For the purposes of this by-law, unless the context otherwise indicates—</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder">account holder</span>" means any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_1">person</span> who is due to receive a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_account" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_2">municipal account</span>, which includes a user of pre-paid electricity or water;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-annual_budget">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-annual_budget">annual budget</span>" means the budget approved by the municipal council for any particular financial year, and includes any adjustments to such budget;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-applicant">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-applicant">applicant</span>" means a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_3">person</span> who applies for the supply of municipal services;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-availability_charge">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-availability_charge">availability data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_4">owner</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_5">property</span> service</span> to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_7" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_7">premises</span>;</span><span class="akn-p" amounts payable arising from any other liability or obligation;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-consumer">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-consumer">consumer</span>" means data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_5__term_2">local community</span> irrespective of whether—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_5__item_a" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_5__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_5__item_a__term_1">municipality</span> through an internal mechanism contemplated in section 76 of the Municipal Systems Act, 2000 or by engaging an external mechanism contemplated in the said section 76; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_5__item_b" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_5__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">fees, charges or tariffs are levied in respect of such a service or not;</span></span></span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_tariff">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_tariff">municipal tariff</span>" means a tariff for on such service;</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_6" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_6" data-refersTo="#term-occupier"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">"<span administrator;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_8__item_d__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_8__item_d__list_1__item_iii"><span data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_8__item_d__list_1__item_iii__term_1">property</span> in an insolvent estate or in liquidation, a trustee or liquidator;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_8__item_d__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_8__item_d__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">in the case of a <span id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_8__item_d__list_1__item_iv__term_2" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_8__item_d__list_1__item_iv__term_2">person</span> under judicial management, a judicial manager;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_8__item_d__list_1__item_v" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_8__item_d__list_1__item_v"><span data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_8__item_d__list_1__item_v__term_1">property</span> in the estate of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_8__item_d__list_1__item_v__term_2" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_8__item_d__list_1__item_v__term_2">person</span> under curatorship, a curator;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_8__item_d__list_1__item_vi" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_8__item_d__list_1__item_vi"><span class="akn-num">(vi)</span><span class="akn-p">in the servitude is registered;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_8__item_d__list_1__item_vii" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_8__item_d__list_1__item_vii"><span class="akn-num">(vii)</span><span class="akn-p">in the case of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_8__item_d__list_1__item_vii__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_8__item_d__list_1__item_vii__term_1">property</span> that is registered in the name of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_8__item_d__list_1__item_vii__term_2" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_8__item_d__list_1__item_vii__term_2">municipality</span> and is leased by it, a lessee; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_8__item_d__list_1__item_viii" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_8__item_d__list_1__item_viii"><span class="akn-num">(viii)</span><span class="akn-p">in the case of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_8__item_d__list_1__item_viii__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_8__item_d__list_1__item_viii__term_1">property</span> sold by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_8__item_d__list_1__item_viii__term_2" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_8__item_d__list_1__item_viii__term_2">municipality</span> and of which possession was given to the buyer pending registration of ownership in the name of such buyer, a buyer;</span></span></span></span></span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-permitted_use">"<span class="akn-def" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_54">property</span>, means the limited purposes for which the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_55" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_55">property</span> may be used in terms of any restrictions imposed by a condition of title, a provision of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_56" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_56">municipality</span>’s town planning or land use scheme, or any legislation applicable to any specific <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_57" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_57">property</span> or properties, or any alleviation of any such restrictions;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-person">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-person">person</span>" includes a legal person and an <span class="akn-term" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_60" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_60">municipality</span>;</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9" data-refersTo="#term-premises"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-premises">premises</span>" means any piece of land, the external surface boundaries of which are delineated on—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_a" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">a general plan or diagram registered in terms of Land Survey, Act of 1927 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1927/9" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1927/9">Act 9 of 1927</a>), or in terms of the Deeds Registry, Act of 1937\(<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1937/47" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1937/47">Act 47 of 1937</a>); or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_b" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">a sectional plan registered in terms of the Sectional Titles Act, 1986 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1986/93" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1986/93">Act 93 of 1986</a>), which is situated within the area of jurisdiction of the municipality;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_c" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_9__item_c"><span data-refersTo="#term-property">property</span>" means—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_10__item_a" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_10__item_a"><span property in the name of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_10__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_10__item_b__term_1">person</span>, but excluding a mortgage bond registered against the property;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_10__item_c" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_10__item_c"><span data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_10__item_c__term_2">person</span> in terms of legislation, such as a "<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-land_reform_beneficiary" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_10__item_c__term_3" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_10__item_c__term_3">land reform beneficiary</span>"; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_10__item_d" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_10__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p"><span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-public_service_infrastructure" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_10__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_10__item_d__term_1">public service infrastructure</span>;</span></span></span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-publicly_controlled">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-publicly_controlled">publicly controlled</span>" services or labour move across a municipal boundary;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_11__item_b" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_11__item_b"><span scheme servicing the public;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_11__item_c" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_11__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span scheme for transporting such fuels;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_11__item_e" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_11__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span public;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_11__item_g" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_11__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">runways or aprons at national or provincial airports;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_11__item_h" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_11__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">breakwaters, seawalls, channels, basins, quay walls, jetties, roads, railway or infrastructure used for the provision of water, lights, power, sewerage or similar services of ports, or navigational aids comprising lighthouses, radio navigational aids, buoys, beacons or any other device or system used to assist the safe and efficient navigation of vessels;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_11__item_i" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_11__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">any other <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-publicly_controlled" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_11__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_11__item_i__term_1">publicly controlled</span> infrastructure as may be prescribed by as law; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_11__item_j" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__list_11__item_j"><span class="akn-num">(j)</span><span class="akn-p">rights of way, easements or servitudes in connection with infrastructure mentioned in paragraphs (a) to (i);</span></span></span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-revenue">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-revenue">revenue</span>" means all monies due to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_62" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_62">municipality</span> and to which the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_63" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_63">municipality</span> has the right to exact and to enforce payment of, irrespective of the reason for or the origin of its factuality;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-sectional_title_scheme">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-sectional_title_scheme">sectional title scheme</span>" means a scheme as 1986</a>);</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-tampering">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-tampering">tampering</span>" means any unauthorised interference with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_64" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_64">municipality</span>’s supply, seals and metering equipment and "tamper" has a corresponding meaning;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-target">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-target">target</span>" means realistic targets which may be set by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_65" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_65">municipality</span> ; and</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-tariffs_for_major_services">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-tariffs_for_major_services">tariffs for major services</span>" means tariffs set for the supply and consumption or usage of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-major_services" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_66" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_66">major services</span>;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-unreliable_customer">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-unreliable_customer">unreliable customer</span>" includes an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_67" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_67">account holder</span>, who according to his or her payment record fails to settle his or her <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_account" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_68" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_68">municipal account</span> by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-due_date" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_69" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_69">due date</span> or who is in arrears with payments due to council or who tampers or interferes with metering equipment, seals or the supply of municipal services.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_1" data-eId="chp_1"><h2>Chapter 1<br>Customer care principles, objectives and implemenatation, and differentitaion</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_2" data-eId="sec_2"><h3>2. Customer care principles, and objectives</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_2__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_2__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_2__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">municipality</span> aims—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_2__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">to move progressively towards the social and economic upliftment of the community in harmony with its natural environment;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_2__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">to provide basic services that are affordable to all its people, and specifically to the poor and disadvantaged, provided that, where applicable, service fees, rates, metered services, other municipal charges, levies, fees, fines, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-interest" id="sec_2__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">interest</span>, taxes or any other amount or amounts payable, arising from any other liability or obligation, are paid for;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_2__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">to engage the active participation of the community in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_2__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">municipality</span>’s affairs, in particular in planning, service delivery and performance management;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_2__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">to provide efficient, effective and transparent administration that conforms to constitutional principles;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_2__subsec_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">to ensure that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_2__subsec_1__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_1__list_1__item_e__term_1">municipality</span> is financially and economically viable; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_2__subsec_1__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_1__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">to create a harmonious relationship between the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_2__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__term_1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_1__list_1__item_f__term_1">municipality</span> and the community through the acknowledgement of reciprocal rights and duties;</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_2__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_2__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2__term_1">municipality</span> by this by-law, designs, regulates on and implements a customer care and management system as contemplated in section 95 of the Municipal Systems Act.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_3" data-eId="sec_3"><h3>3. Municipal manager responsible <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-officer" id="sec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_3__term_1">officer</span>
</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_manager" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1">municipal manager</span>—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">is responsible to the Executive Mayor for the implementation and enforcement of the provisions of this by-law;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">must, for the purposes of paragraph (a) take the necessary steps to implement and enforce the provisions of this by-law;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">is accountable to the Executive Mayor for the agreed performance targets as approved by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__term_1">municipality</span> and the Executive Mayor, and for these purposes must—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__list_1" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">report to the Executive Mayor on matters relating to this by-law, including but not limited to—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_aa" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_aa"><span class="akn-num">(aa)</span><span class="akn-p">the effectiveness of administrative mechanisms, resources processes and procedures to collect money that is due and payable to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_aa__term_1" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_aa__term_1">municipality</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_bb" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_bb"><span class="akn-num">(bb)</span><span class="akn-p"><span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-billing" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_bb__term_1" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_bb__term_1">billing</span> information, including the number of account holders, accruals, cash-flow, and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-customer_management" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_bb__term_2" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_bb__term_2">customer management</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_cc" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_cc"><span class="akn-num">(cc)</span><span class="akn-p">the satisfaction levels of account holders regarding services rendered; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_dd" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_dd"><span class="akn-num">(dd)</span><span class="akn-p">the effectiveness of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_dd__term_1" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_i__list_1__item_dd__term_1">municipality</span>’s indigence relief measures; and</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">encourage and bear on account holders, where needed, to settle outstanding accounts within the ambit of this by-law; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii__list_1" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">with the consent of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii__list_1__term_1">account holder</span>, enter into an agreement with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii__list_1__term_2">account holder</span>’s employer to deduct from the salary or wages of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii__list_1__term_3">account holder</span>—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii__list_1__item_aa" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii__list_1__item_aa"><span class="akn-num">(aa)</span><span class="akn-p">any outstanding amounts as may be agreed; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii__list_1__item_bb" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__list_1__item_iii__list_1__item_bb"><span class="akn-num">(bb)</span><span class="akn-p">such regular monthly amounts as may be agreed, and may provide special incentives for employers to enter into such agreements, and employees to consent to such agreements.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_4" data-eId="sec_4"><h3>4. Differentiation between customers and exemption</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_4__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">In accordance with the principles embodied in the <a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1996/constitution" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1996/constitution">Constitution</a> and sections 74(3) and 75 of the Local Government: Municipal Systems Act, 2000, the municipality may differentiate between different categories of users and consumers in regard to the tariffs which it levies, categories of ratepayers, account holders, customers, debtors, taxes, services, service standards and other matters, however, such differentiation must at all times be reasonable, and must be fully disclosed in each annual budget.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_4__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">municipality</span> may, in writing exempt an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__term_2">account holder</span>, category of account holders, or other persons from complying with a provision of this by-law, subject to any conditions it may impose, if the application or operation of that provision would be unreasonable, however the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__term_3">municipality</span> or its authorised agent may not grant exemption from any section of this by-law that may result in—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the wastage or excessive consumption of water or electricity;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the evasion or avoidance of water or electricity restrictions;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">significant negative effects on public health, safety or the environment;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">the non-payment for services;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">the installation of pipes and fittings which are not acceptable in terms of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_e__term_1">municipality</span>’s prescribed standard; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">any Act, or any regulation made under it, not being complied with.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_4__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_4__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_3__term_1">municipality</span> or its authorised agent may at any time after giving written notice of at least 30 days, withdraw any exemption given under subsection (2).</span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_2" data-eId="chp_2"><h2>Chapter 2<br>Supply of municipal services</h2>
<section class="akn-part" id="chp_2__part_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_1"><h2>Part 1 – Application for supply and service agreements, credit screening, deposits, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-billing" id="chp_2__part_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_2__part_1__term_1">billing</span> and payment, and termination of service agreements</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_5" data-eId="sec_5"><h3>5. Application for supply of municipal services and service agreements</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_5__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any application for any supply of services to any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_5__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1__term_1">premises</span> must be made at the municipal offices at least four working days, or such lesser period as may be accepted by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_5__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1__term_2">municipality</span>, prior to the service being required and must comply with the conditions determined by the Municipal Manager.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_5__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">After the commencement of this by-law only the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_5__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_2__term_1">owner</span> of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_5__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_2__term_2">property</span> or a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_5__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_2__term_3">person</span> who has written authority from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_5__subsec_2__term_4" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_2__term_4">owner</span>, may apply for municipal services to be supplied to a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_5__subsec_2__term_5" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_2__term_5">property</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_5__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No services shall be supplied unless and until application has been made by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_5__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_3__term_1">owner</span> and a service agreement in the format prescribed by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_5__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_3__term_2">municipality</span> has been entered into and a deposit provided for in section 6 has been paid.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_5__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Upon receipt of an application for services the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_5__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_4__term_1">municipality</span> must notify the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_5__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_4__term_2">applicant</span> of the different levels of services and the tariffs payable in respect of each level of service.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_5__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_5__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_5__term_1">municipality</span> shall only be responsible to provide a specific level of services if it already provides such level of services in the ordinary run of matters and if it has the capacity to provide such level of services.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_5__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_5__subsec_6__list_1" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_6__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Where the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_5__subsec_6__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_6__list_1__term_1">municipality</span>—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_5__subsec_6__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_6__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">refuses to provide a specific level of services;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_5__subsec_6__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_6__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">is not in a position to provide such a level of service on the date it is requested;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_5__subsec_6__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_6__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">is not in a position whatsoever to provide such a level of service, it must notify the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_5__subsec_6__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_6__list_1__item_c__term_1">applicant</span> within a reasonable time of its inability to provide the service, the reasons therefor and if applicable, when the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_5__subsec_6__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_6__list_1__item_c__term_2">municipality</span> will be in a position to provide such service.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_6" data-eId="sec_6"><h3>6. Deposits</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_6__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">On approval of the application and before the service is made available, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">municipality</span> may require the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">applicant</span>—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">to deposit for municipal services with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">municipality</span> a sum of money;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">to provide any other form of security; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">to agree to special conditions regarding payment of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_account" id="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">municipal account</span>, and monies so deposited with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_2">municipality</span> serve as security.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_6__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The amount payable as deposit shall be determine as part of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_6__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_2__term_1">municipality</span>’s tariff policy and may be determined for different kinds of consumers.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_6__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The director: Financial Services may, in respect of preferred clients, grant a relaxation of the conditions applicable to deposits as contemplated in subsections (1) and (2), and may in the case of services being suspended or restricted, decide to increase the deposit for re-connection.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_6__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Upon the suspension of services, the deposit, minus any payments due to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_6__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_4__term_1">municipality</span>, must be refunded to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_6__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_4__term_2">account holder</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_6__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_6__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_5__term_1">municipality</span> is not liable for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-interest" id="sec_6__subsec_5__term_2" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_5__term_2">interest</span> payable on deposits held.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_7" data-eId="sec_7"><h3>7. Billing and payment</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_7__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_7__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_1__term_1">account holder</span> must pay all amounts due to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_7__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_1__term_2">municipality</span> as reflected in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_account" id="sec_7__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_1__term_3">municipal account</span>, and the onus is on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_7__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_1__term_4">account holder</span> to verify the accuracy of such account.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_7__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_7__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_2__term_1">account holder</span> must pay for metered services, and must pay the rates, other municipal charges, levies, fees, fines, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-interest" id="sec_7__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_2__term_2">interest</span>, taxes or any other liability or obligation from the date of origin of such municipal charges until the written termination of the services.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_7__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__term_1">account holder</span>—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">must, where possible, be rendered one account, on which the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-due_date" id="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1">due date</span> for settlement of the total amount owing is reflected, subject to the provisions of subsection (14); and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">must be billed monthly in cycles of approximately 30 days.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_7__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Payment must be received on or before the close of business on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-due_date" id="sec_7__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_4__term_1">due date</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_7__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Payment made via electronic media or any of the service providers appointed by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_7__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_5__term_1">municipality</span> to receive payments on its behalf, should be made at least four working days before the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-due_date" id="sec_7__subsec_5__term_2" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_5__term_2">due date</span> to enable the payment to be processed, and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-interest" id="sec_7__subsec_5__term_3" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_5__term_3">interest</span> accrues should the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_7__subsec_5__term_4" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_5__term_4">municipality</span> receive payment after the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-due_date" id="sec_7__subsec_5__term_5" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_5__term_5">due date</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_7__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_7__subsec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_6__term_1">account holder</span> effects payment of an account via a service provider four working days or more before the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-due_date" id="sec_7__subsec_6__term_2" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_6__term_2">due date</span> and such service provider fails to furnish the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_7__subsec_6__term_3" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_6__term_3">municipality</span> with the relevant payment details, such service provider may be held liable for all charges incurred by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_7__subsec_6__term_4" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_6__term_4">municipality</span> to recover an arrear amount erroneously reflected on the account of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_7__subsec_6__term_5" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_6__term_5">account holder</span>, as well as for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-interest" id="sec_7__subsec_6__term_6" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_6__term_6">interest</span> charges.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_7__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_7__subsec_7__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_7__term_1">municipality</span> may estimate the quantity of metered services supplied in respect of a period or periods within the interval between actual successive readings of the meters, which intervals may not exceed 4months, and may render an account to an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_7__subsec_7__term_2" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_7__term_2">account holder</span> for the quantity of metered services so estimated.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_7__subsec_8" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_8"><span class="akn-num">(8)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_7__subsec_8__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_8__term_1">account holder</span> is dissatisfied with an account rendered for metered services supplied by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_7__subsec_8__term_2" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_8__term_2">municipality</span>, such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_7__subsec_8__term_3" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_8__term_3">account holder</span> may, prior to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-due_date" id="sec_7__subsec_8__term_4" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_8__term_4">due date</span> stipulated therein object to the account, setting out reasons for such dissatisfaction.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_7__subsec_9" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_9"><span class="akn-num">(9)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Should any dispute arise as to the amount owing by an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_7__subsec_9__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_9__term_1">account holder</span>, and subject to the provisions of section 102 of the Local Government: Municipal Systems Act, 2000 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/2000/32" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/2000/32">Act 32 of 2000</a>), the account holder must notwithstanding such dispute proceed to make regular payments by the due date based on the calculation of the average municipal account for the preceding three months prior to the arising of the dispute and taking into account interest as well as the annual amendments of tariffs of the municipality.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_7__subsec_10" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_10"><span class="akn-num">(10)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An error or omission in any account or failure to render an account does not relieve the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_7__subsec_10__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_10__term_1">account holder</span> of the obligation to pay by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-due_date" id="sec_7__subsec_10__term_2" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_10__term_2">due date</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_7__subsec_11" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_11"><span class="akn-num">(11)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_7__subsec_11__list_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_11__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">If an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_7__subsec_11__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_11__list_1__term_1">account holder</span> uses water or electricity for a category of use other than that for which it is supplied by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_7__subsec_11__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_11__list_1__term_2">municipality</span> and is in consequence not charged for water or electricity so used, or is charged for the water or electricity at a rate lower than that at which the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_7__subsec_11__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_11__list_1__term_3">account holder</span> should be charged, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_7__subsec_11__list_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_11__list_1__term_4">account holder</span> is liable for the amount due to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_7__subsec_11__list_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_11__list_1__term_5">municipality</span> in accordance with the prescribed charges in respect of—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_7__subsec_11__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_11__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the quantity of water or electricity which the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_7__subsec_11__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_11__list_1__item_a__term_1">account holder</span> has used and for which the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_7__subsec_11__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_11__list_1__item_a__term_2">account holder</span> has not been charged; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_7__subsec_11__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_11__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the difference between the cost of the water or electricity used by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_7__subsec_11__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_11__list_1__item_b__term_1">account holder</span> at the rate at which the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_7__subsec_11__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_11__list_1__item_b__term_2">account holder</span> has been charged and the cost of the water or electricity at the rate at which the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_7__subsec_11__list_1__item_b__term_3" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_11__list_1__item_b__term_3">account holder</span> should have been charged.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_7__subsec_12" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_12"><span class="akn-num">(12)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_7__subsec_12__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_12__term_1">account holder</span> is not entitled to a reduction of the amount payable for metered services which are lost due to a fault in the meter, until such time as the provisions of section 13(8)(c) have been met.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_7__subsec_13" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_13"><span class="akn-num">(13)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_7__subsec_13__list_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_13__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_7__subsec_13__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_13__list_1__term_1">municipality</span> may—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_7__subsec_13__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_13__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">consolidate any separate accounts of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_7__subsec_13__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_13__list_1__item_a__term_1">account holder</span> liable for payment to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_7__subsec_13__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_13__list_1__item_a__term_2">municipality</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_7__subsec_13__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_13__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">credit any payment by an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_7__subsec_13__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_13__list_1__item_b__term_1">account holder</span> against any debt of that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_7__subsec_13__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_13__list_1__item_b__term_2">account holder</span>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_7__subsec_14" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_14"><span class="akn-num">(14)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_7__subsec_14__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_14__term_1">owner</span> of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_7__subsec_14__term_2" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_14__term_2">property</span> may enter into an agreement with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_7__subsec_14__term_3" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_14__term_3">municipality</span> in terms of which payment for rates is made annually, in which case payment must be made on or before the date determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_7__subsec_14__term_4" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_14__term_4">municipality</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_7__subsec_15" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_15"><span class="akn-num">(15)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where an account is not paid in full, any lesser amount offered and accepted by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_7__subsec_15__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_15__term_1">municipality</span>, shall not be regarded as full and final settlement of the account, unless the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_manager" id="sec_7__subsec_15__term_2" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_15__term_2">municipal manager</span> has accepted in writing such payment as full and final settlement of the account.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_7__subsec_16" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_16"><span class="akn-num">(16)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_7__subsec_16__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_16__term_1">municipality</span> undertakes to provide and maintain strategically situated payment offices and cashiers throughout the municipal area.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_8" data-eId="sec_8"><h3>8. Termination of service agreement</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_8__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Termination of the service agreement must be in writing to the other party of the intention to do so.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_8__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_8__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_2__term_1">property</span> is sold, an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_8__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_2__term_2">owner</span> may terminate a service agreement by giving the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_8__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_2__term_3">municipality</span> not less than four working days’ notice in writing.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_8__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__term_1">municipality</span> may, by notice in writing of not less than 14 working days, advise an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__term_2">account holder</span> of the termination of the agreement for a supply of municipal services if—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1">account holder</span> has committed a breach of this by-law and has failed to rectify such breach; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1">municipality</span> cannot continue to supply the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_2">account holder</span> with municipal services, as in terms of an arrangement with another authority supplying municipal services such authority must in future supply municipal services to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_3" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_3">account holder</span>.</span></span></span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_2__part_2" data-eId="chp_2__part_2"><h2>Part 2 – Non-payment of municipal accounts</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_9" data-eId="sec_9"><h3>9. Arrangements for payments</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_9__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Should an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_9__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_1__term_1">account holder</span>, before any of the steps have been taken in terms of section 11, not be able to pay the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_account" id="sec_9__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_1__term_2">municipal account</span> in full, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_9__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_1__term_3">account holder</span> may approach the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_9__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_1__term_4">municipality</span> with the aim of making short-term arrangements to settle the account.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_9__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Should an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_9__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_2__term_1">account holder</span>, after any of the steps have been taken in terms of section 13, experience difficulties in paying the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_account" id="sec_9__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_2__term_2">municipal account</span>, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_9__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_2__term_3">account holder</span> may approach the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_9__subsec_2__term_4" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_2__term_4">municipality</span> with the aim of making arrangements to settle the account, and the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_9__subsec_2__term_5" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_2__term_5">account holder</span> must enter into a written agreement with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_9__subsec_2__term_6" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_2__term_6">municipality</span> to repay to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_9__subsec_2__term_7" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_2__term_7">municipality</span> the outstanding and due amount under the conditions and on a basis determined, by the Municipal Manager,.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_9__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The written agreement must be signed on behalf of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_9__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_3__term_1">municipality</span> by a duly authorised <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-officer" id="sec_9__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_3__term_2">officer</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_9__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_9__subsec_4__list_1" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_4__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">In the instance where arrangements for payment have been made the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_9__subsec_4__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_4__list_1__term_1">municipality</span> may—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_9__subsec_4__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_4__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">review the deposit;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_9__subsec_4__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_4__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">require of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_9__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_1">account holder</span> to pay by means of a stop order or debit order;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_9__subsec_4__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_4__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">require of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_9__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__term_1">account holder</span> to convert to a pre-paid metering system; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_9__subsec_4__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_4__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">require any other form of security, including personal suretyship by the directors or members of a company, closed corporation, trust or body corporate.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_10" data-eId="sec_10"><h3>10. Interest on overdue municipal accounts</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_10__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_10__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_1__term_1">municipality</span> may, charge or recover <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-interest" id="sec_10__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_1__term_2">interest</span> at a rate determined by it in respect of any arrear amounts due and payable.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_10__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Irrespective of the reason for non-payment, or where an arrangement has been made in terms of section 9, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-interest" id="sec_10__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_2__term_1">interest</span> accrues if an account is unpaid.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_10__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Interest is calculated monthly according to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-interest" id="sec_10__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_3__term_1">interest</span> rate approved by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_10__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_3__term_2">municipality</span>, and a portion of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-month" id="sec_10__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_3__term_3">month</span> is regarded as a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-month" id="sec_10__subsec_3__term_4" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_3__term_4">month</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_10__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Interest is payable if payment is not received at an office of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_10__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_4__term_1">municipality</span> or to the credit of the bank account of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_10__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_4__term_2">municipality</span> at the close of business on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-due_date" id="sec_10__subsec_4__term_3" data-eId="sec_10__subsec_4__term_3">due date</span>.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_11" data-eId="sec_11"><h3>11. Debt collection mechanisms</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_11__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Where appropriate, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">municipality</span> must at all times attempt to advise an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">account holder</span> of an impending disconnection or restriction of a supply, and the following mechanisms may be applied should an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__term_3">account holder</span> fail to settle a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_account" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__term_4">municipal account</span> by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-due_date" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__term_5">due date</span>:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">delivering or mailing of a final demand and explaining to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">account holder</span> the status of the account and the consequences of not paying or concluding an arrangement;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">informing the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">account holder</span> verbally, in writing, telephonically, or by electronic means of the overdue amount and the impending disconnection or restriction of services;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">disconnecting or restricting the supply of municipal services to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">premises</span> and the serving of a disconnection or restriction notice on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_2">account holder</span>; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">debiting the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_account" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1">municipal account</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_2" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_2">account holder</span> with all relevant fees or penalties approved by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_3" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_3">municipality</span>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_11__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Where the water- or electricity supply had been disconnected in terms of this section, such supply shall be re-connected only when—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">all amounts due plus <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-interest" id="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">interest</span> are paid in full or an agreement for settlement has been entered into in terms of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_2">municipality</span>’s Credit control and Debt Collection Policy; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the fees for disconnection or re-connection as determined in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">municipality</span>’s Tariff Policy has been paid.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_11__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_11__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Where the metered usage is discontinued or restricted and the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_11__subsec_3__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_3__list_1__term_1">account holder</span> remains in default of payment, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_11__subsec_3__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_3__list_1__term_2">premises</span> may visited at regular intervals to ensure that metered supply remains discontinued or restricted and where it is found that such services have been re-connected, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_11__subsec_3__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_3__list_1__term_3">municipality</span> shall have the right to—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">take the steps required in terms of section 31, in which case the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_11__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1">account holder</span> remains responsible for the charges or costs for damages incurred;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">refuse to provide services for a period determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_11__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1">municipality</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_3__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_3__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">in the case of a pre-payment meter, to terminated further selling of prepaid services.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_11__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where a duly authorised <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-officer" id="sec_11__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_4__term_1">officer</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_11__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_4__term_2">municipality</span> has visited the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_11__subsec_4__term_3" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_4__term_3">premises</span> for the purpose of disconnecting or restricting the supply and was obstructed or prevented from effecting such disconnection or restriction, an amount equal to the prescribed fee for a reconnection becomes payable for each visit necessary for the purpose of such disconnection or restriction, subject to a maximum of two such visits during which disconnection or restriction could not be effected.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_11__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__term_1">municipality</span> may use any one or more of the following mechanisms to secure full payment of any amounts owing to it:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">requiring of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__item_a__term_1">account holder</span> to convert to another metering system;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">allocating a portion of any pre-paid payment to other debts;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">publishing a list of account holders who remain in default;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">withholding payment of a grant-in-aid and subject to the provisions of section 30, excluding the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__item_d__term_1">account holder</span> from the tender process;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">withholding payment on contracts for settlement of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_account" id="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__item_e__term_1">municipal account</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">reviewing and altering the conditions of the service agreement;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">instituting legal proceedings for the recovery of the debt;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__item_h" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">classifying the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__item_h__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__item_h__term_1">account holder</span> as an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-unreliable_customer" id="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__item_h__term_2" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__item_h__term_2">unreliable
