customer</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">using the services of external debt collection specialists or agencies;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__item_j" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__item_j"><span class="akn-num">(j)</span><span class="akn-p">insisting on conversion to pre-paid metering at the cost of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__item_j__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__item_j__term_1">account holder</span>; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__item_k" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__item_k"><span class="akn-num">(k)</span><span class="akn-p">employing any other methods authorised by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__item_k__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_5__list_1__item_k__term_1">municipality</span> from time to time to recover arrear amounts.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_11__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The cost of collection, where applicable, is for the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_11__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_5__term_1">account holder</span>’s account.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_11__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_11__subsec_6__list_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_6__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Subject to the provisions of sections 28 and 29 of the Property Rates Act, 2004 <a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/2004/6" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/2004/6">Act 6 of 2004</a>), the right to deny, restrict, disconnect or terminate services due to the non-payment for any rates, metered services, other municipal charges, levies, fees, fines, interest, taxes or any other amount or amounts payable arising from any other liability or obligation prevails notwithstanding the fact that—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_6__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_6__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">payment was intended for any specific service; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_6__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_6__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_11__subsec_6__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_6__list_1__item_b__term_1">person</span> who entered into a service agreement for supply of services with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_11__subsec_6__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_6__list_1__item_b__term_2">municipality</span> and the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_11__subsec_6__list_1__item_b__term_3" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_6__list_1__item_b__term_3">owner</span> are different entities or persons, as the case may be.</span></span></span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_2__part_3" data-eId="chp_2__part_3"><h2>Part 3 – Metering equipment and metering of services</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_12" data-eId="sec_12"><h3>12. General provisions</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_12__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_12__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_12__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_12__hcontainer_1__term_1">municipality</span> may introduce various metering equipment and may encourage an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_12__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_12__hcontainer_1__term_2">account holder</span> to convert to a system which will benefit the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_12__hcontainer_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_12__hcontainer_1__term_3">municipality</span> and account holders.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_13" data-eId="sec_13"><h3>13. Metering equipment and measuring of consumption</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_1__term_1">municipality</span> must, at the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_13__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_1__term_2">consumer</span>’s cost in the form of a direct charge or prescribed fee, provide, install and maintain appropriately rated metering equipment at the point of metering for measuring metered services.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_2__term_1">municipality</span> reserves the right to meter the supply to a block of shops, flats, tenement-houses and similar buildings for the building as a whole, or for an individual unit, or for a group of units.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Where any building referred to in subsection (2) is metered by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__term_1">municipality</span> as a whole —</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1">owner</span> may, at own cost, provide and install appropriate sub-metering equipment for each shop, flat and tenement; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1">municipality</span> may require the installation, at the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_2">account holder</span>’s expense, of a meter for each unit of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_3" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_3">premises</span> in separate occupation for the purpose of determining the quantity of metered services supplied to each such unit.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where the electricity used by consumers is charged at different tariffs, the consumption must be metered separately for each tariff.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where sub-metering equipment is installed, accommodation separate from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_5__term_1">municipality</span>’s metering equipment must be provided where appropriate.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Except in the case of pre-payment meters, the quantity of metered services used by a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_13__subsec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_6__term_1">consumer</span> during any metering period is ascertained by reading the appropriate meter or meters supplied and installed by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_6__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_6__term_2">municipality</span> at the beginning and end of such metering period, except where the metering equipment is found to be defective.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">For the purpose of calculating the amount due and payable for the quantity of metered services consumed, the same amount of metered services is deemed to be consumed during every period of 24 hours between readings.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_8" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_8"><span class="akn-num">(8)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_13__subsec_8__list_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_8__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The following apply to the accuracy of metering:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_8__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_8__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">a meter is conclusively presumed to be registering accurately if its error, when tested in the manner prescribed in subsection (13), is found to be within the limits of error as provided for in the applicable standard specifications;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_8__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_8__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_13__subsec_8__list_1__item_b__list_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_8__list_1__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_8__list_1__item_b__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_8__list_1__item_b__list_1__term_1">municipality</span> has the right to test its metering equipment, and if it is established by test or otherwise that such metering equipment is defective, the Municipality must—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_8__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_8__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">in case of a credit meter, adjust the account rendered; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_8__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_8__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_13__subsec_8__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__list_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_8__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">in the case of prepayment meters:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_8__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__list_1__item_aa" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_8__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__list_1__item_aa"><span class="akn-num">(aa)</span><span class="akn-p">render an account where the meter has been under-registering; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_8__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__list_1__item_bb" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_8__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__list_1__item_bb"><span class="akn-num">(bb)</span><span class="akn-p">issue a free token where the meter has been over-registering; and</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_8__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_8__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_13__subsec_8__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_8__list_1__item_c__term_1">consumer</span> is entitled to have the metering equipment tested by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_8__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_8__list_1__item_c__term_2">municipality</span> on payment of the prescribed fee, and if the metering equipment is found not to comply with the system accuracy requirements as provided for in the applicable standard specifications, an adjustment in accordance with the provisions of paragraph (b) and subsection (7) must be made and the aforesaid fee must be refunded.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_9" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_9"><span class="akn-num">(9)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No alterations, repairs, additions or connections of any description may be made on the supply side of the point of metering unless specifically approved in writing by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_manager" id="sec_13__subsec_9__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_9__term_1">municipal manager</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_10" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_10"><span class="akn-num">(10)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Prior to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__term_1">municipality</span> making any upward adjustment to an account in terms of subsection (8)(b), the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__term_2">municipality</span> must—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">notify the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_a__term_1">consumer</span> in writing of the monetary value of the adjustment to be made and the reasons therefor;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">in such notification provide sufficient particulars to enable the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_b__term_1">consumer</span> to submit representations thereon; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">call upon the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_c__term_1">consumer</span> in such notice to present it with reasons in writing, if any, within 21 days or such longer period as the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_c__term_2">municipality</span> may permit, why the account should not be adjusted as notified, and should the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_c__term_3" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_c__term_3">consumer</span> fail to provide any representation during the period the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_c__term_4" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_c__term_4">municipality</span> is entitled to adjust the account as notified in paragraph (a).</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_11" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_11"><span class="akn-num">(11)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_11__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_11__term_1">municipality</span> must consider any representation provided by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_13__subsec_11__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_11__term_2">consumer</span> in terms of subsection (10) and may adjust the account appropriately.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_12" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_12"><span class="akn-num">(12)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If the Municipal Manager decides that such representation does not establish a case warranting an amendment to the monetary value established in terms of subsection (15), the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_12__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_12__term_1">municipality</span> is entitled to adjust the account as notified in terms of subsection (10)(a), and the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_13__subsec_12__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_12__term_2">consumer</span> has the right to appeal the decision of the official in terms of section 62 of the Local Government: Municipal Systems Act, 2000 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/2000/32" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/2000/32">Act 32 of 2000</a>).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_13" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_13"><span class="akn-num">(13)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Meters are tested in the manner provided for in the applicable standard specifications.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_14" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_14"><span class="akn-num">(14)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">When an adjustment is made to the consumption registered on a meter in terms of subsection (8)(b) or (8)(c), such adjustment is based either on the percentage error of the meter as determined by the test referred to in subsection (13), or upon a calculation by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_14__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_14__term_1">municipality</span> from consumption data in its possession, and where applicable, due allowance must be made, where possible, for seasonal or other variations which may affect consumption.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_15" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_15"><span class="akn-num">(15)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">When an adjustment is made as contemplated in subsection (14), the adjustment may not exceed a period of six months preceding the date on which the metering equipment was found to be inaccurate, however the application of this subsection does not bar a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_13__subsec_15__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_15__term_1">consumer</span> from claiming back overpayment for any longer period where the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_13__subsec_15__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_15__term_2">consumer</span> is able to prove the claim in the normal legal process.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_16" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_16"><span class="akn-num">(16)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_13__subsec_16__list_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_16__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_16__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_16__list_1__term_1">municipality</span> may dispense with the use of a meter in case of—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_16__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_16__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">an automatic sprinkler fire installation; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_16__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_16__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">special circumstances that may justify such dispensation.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_17" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_17"><span class="akn-num">(17)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_13__subsec_17__list_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_17__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_17__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_17__list_1__term_1">municipality</span> may by notice—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_17__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_17__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_13__subsec_17__list_1__item_a__list_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_17__list_1__item_a__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">prohibit or restrict the consumption of metered services—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_17__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_17__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">for specified or non-specified purposes;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_17__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_17__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">during specified hours of the day or on specified days or otherwise than during specified hours of the day or on specified days; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_17__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_17__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">in a specified or non-specified manner; and</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_17__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_17__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_13__subsec_17__list_1__item_b__list_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_17__list_1__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">determine and impose—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_17__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_17__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">limits on the quantity of metered services which may be consumed over a specified period;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_17__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_17__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">charges additional to those prescribed in respect of the supply of metered services in excess of a limit contemplated in subparagraph (i) ; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_17__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_17__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">a general surcharge on the prescribed charges in respect of the supply of metered services; and</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_17__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_17__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">impose restrictions or prohibitions on the use or manner of use or disposition of an appliance by means of which metered services is used or consumed, or on the connection of such appliance.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_18" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_18"><span class="akn-num">(18)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_18__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_18__term_1">municipality</span> may limit the application of the provisions of a notice contemplated by subsection (17) to specified areas and classes of account holders, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_13__subsec_18__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_18__term_2">premises</span> and activities, and may provide for the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_18__term_3" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_18__term_3">municipality</span> to permit deviations and exemptions from, and the relaxation of any of the provisions.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_19" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_19"><span class="akn-num">(19)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">To ensure compliance with a notice published in terms of subsection (17), the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_19__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_19__term_1">municipality</span> may take, or by written notice require an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_13__subsec_19__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_19__term_2">account holder</span> at the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_13__subsec_19__term_3" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_19__term_3">account holder</span>’s expense to take, such measures, including the installation of measuring devices and devices for restricting the flow of metered services as may be necessary.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_20" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_20"><span class="akn-num">(20)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">In addition to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_13__subsec_20__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_20__term_1">person</span> by whose act or omission a contravention of or failure to comply with the terms of a notice published in terms of subsection (17) is actually committed, an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_13__subsec_20__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_20__term_2">account holder</span> in respect of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_13__subsec_20__term_3" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_20__term_3">premises</span> to which metered services are supplied is presumed also to have committed the contravention or to have so failed to comply, unless evidence is adduced that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_13__subsec_20__term_4" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_20__term_4">account holder</span> had taken all reasonable steps to prevent such a contravention or failure to comply by any other <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_13__subsec_20__term_5" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_20__term_5">person</span>, however, the fact that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_13__subsec_20__term_6" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_20__term_6">account holder</span> issued instructions to the other <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_13__subsec_20__term_7" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_20__term_7">person</span> shall not of itself be accepted as sufficient proof that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_13__subsec_20__term_8" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_20__term_8">account holder</span> took all such reasonable steps.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_21" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_21"><span class="akn-num">(21)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The provisions of this section also apply in respect of metered services supplied directly by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_21__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_21__term_1">municipality</span> to account holders outside its area of jurisdiction, notwithstanding anything to the contrary in the conditions governing such supply, unless otherwise specified in the notice published in terms of subsection (17).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_22" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_22"><span class="akn-num">(22)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_13__subsec_22__list_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_22__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">If action is necessary as a matter of urgency to prevent waste of metered services, refuse or sewerage, damage to <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_13__subsec_22__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_22__list_1__term_1">property</span>, danger to life, or pollution of water, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_22__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_22__list_1__term_2">municipality</span> may—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_22__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_22__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">without prior notice disconnect the supply of metered services to any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_13__subsec_22__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_22__list_1__item_a__term_1">premises</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_22__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_22__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">enter upon such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_13__subsec_22__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_22__list_1__item_b__term_1">premises</span> and do emergency work, as it may deem necessary, and in addition by written notice require the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_13__subsec_22__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_22__list_1__item_b__term_2">account holder</span> to do within a specified period such further work as the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_22__list_1__item_b__term_3" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_22__list_1__item_b__term_3">municipality</span> may deem necessary.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_23" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_23"><span class="akn-num">(23)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_23__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_23__term_1">municipality</span> may recover from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_13__subsec_23__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_23__term_2">account holder</span> the cost of any work undertaken in terms of subsection (22)(b) where such work was undertaken because of an unlawful act or omission by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_13__subsec_23__term_3" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_23__term_3">account holder</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_24" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_24"><span class="akn-num">(24)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Before any metered or pre-paid metered supplies which have been disconnected or restricted for non-payment is restored, an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_13__subsec_24__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_24__term_1">account holder</span> must pay all fees and charges as determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_24__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_24__term_2">municipality</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_25" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_25"><span class="akn-num">(25)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_13__subsec_25__list_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_25__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_25__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_25__list_1__term_1">municipality</span> may, at the written request of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_13__subsec_25__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_25__list_1__term_2">account holder</span> and on the dates requested by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_13__subsec_25__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_25__list_1__term_3">account holder</span>—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_25__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_25__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">disconnect the supply of metered services to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_13__subsec_25__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_25__list_1__item_a__term_1">account holder</span>’s <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_13__subsec_25__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_25__list_1__item_a__term_2">premises</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_25__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_25__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">upon payment of the prescribed charge for restoration, restore the supply of such services.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_26" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_26"><span class="akn-num">(26)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">After disconnection for non-payment of an account or a contravention of any provision of this by-law, the prescribed fees must be paid before reconnection is made.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_27" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_27"><span class="akn-num">(27)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The following apply to the reading of credit meters:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">unless otherwise prescribed, credit meters are normally read at intervals of approximately one <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-month" id="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_a__term_1">month</span> and the fixed or minimum charges due in terms of the tariff are assessed accordingly and the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_a__term_2">municipality</span> is not obliged to effect any adjustments to such charges;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">if for any reason the credit meter cannot be read, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_b__term_1">municipality</span> may render an estimated account, and estimated consumption must be adjusted in a subsequent account in accordance with the consumption actually consumed;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">when an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_c__term_1">account holder</span> vacates a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_c__term_2">property</span> and a final reading of the meter is not possible, an estimation of the consumption may be made and the final account rendered accordingly;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">if a special reading of the meter is desired by a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_d__term_1">consumer</span>, this may be obtained upon payment of the prescribed fee; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_e__list_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_e__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">if any calculating, reading or metering error is discovered in respect of any account rendered to a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_e__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_e__list_1__term_1">consumer</span>—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">the error must be corrected in subsequent accounts;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">any such correction applies only in respect of accounts for a period of six months preceding the date on which the error in the accounts was discovered,</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">the correction is based on the actual tariffs applicable during the period; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">the application of this section does not prevent a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_iv__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_iv__term_1">consumer</span> from claiming back overpayment for any longer period where the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_iv__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_27__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_iv__term_2">consumer</span> is able to prove the claim in the normal legal process.</span></span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_28" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_28"><span class="akn-num">(28)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The following apply to prepayment metering:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">no refund of the amount tendered for the purchase of electricity or water credit is given at the point of sale after initiation of the process by which the pre-payment meter token is produced; provided that this section will only apply to Standard Transfer Specification equipment (STS tokens);</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">copies of previously issued tokens for the transfer of credit to the pre-payment meter may be issued at the request of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_b__term_1">consumer</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">when an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_c__term_1">account holder</span> vacates any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_c__term_2">premises</span> where a pre-payment meter is installed, no refund for the credit remaining in the meter is made to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_c__term_3" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_c__term_3">owner</span> by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_c__term_4" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_c__term_4">municipality</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_d__term_1">municipality</span> is not liable for the re-instatement of credit in a prepayment meter lost due to <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-tampering" id="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_d__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_d__term_2">tampering</span> with, or the incorrect use or the abuse of, pre-payment meters or tokens;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">where an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_e__term_1">account holder</span> is indebted to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_e__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_e__term_2">municipality</span> for any rates, metered services, other municipal charges, levies, fees, fines, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-interest" id="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_e__term_3" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_e__term_3">interest</span>, taxes or any other amount or amounts payable arising from any other liability or obligation, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_e__term_4" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_e__term_4">municipality</span> may deduct a percentage from the amount tendered to offset the amount owing to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_e__term_5" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_e__term_5">municipality</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_f__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_28__list_1__item_f__term_1">municipality</span> may appoint vendors for the sale of credit for prepayment meters and does not guarantee the continued operation of any vendor.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_14" data-eId="sec_14"><h3>14. Resale of water or electricity</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_14__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_14__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_1__term_1">account holder</span> who is supplied with metered services in terms of this by-law may sell or supply water or electricity to any other <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_14__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_1__term_2">person</span> or persons for such use upon any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_14__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_1__term_3">premises</span> other than those in respect of which such agreement is made, or permit or offer such resale or supply to be made, unless prior permission from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_14__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_1__term_4">municipality</span> has been obtained.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_14__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_14__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_2__term_1">municipality</span> grants the permission referred to in subsection (1), it may stipulate the maximum price at which the water or electricity may be sold and impose such other conditions as it may deem fit.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_14__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Permission referred to in subsection (1) may be withdrawn at any time.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_14__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where water or electricity is resold for use on the same <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_14__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_4__term_1">premises</span>, such resale must be in accordance with the tariff and subject to such conditions as the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_14__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_14__subsec_4__term_2">municipality</span> may impose.</span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_2__part_4" data-eId="chp_2__part_4"><h2>Part 4 – Indigence relief measures</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_15" data-eId="sec_15"><h3>15. Requirements for indigence relief</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_15__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">To qualify for indigence relief, the following requirements must be met:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">applicant</span> must be an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2">account holder</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__term_1">applicant</span> must, before a date determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__term_2">municipality</span>, apply annually, or at such intervals as determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__term_3">municipality</span>, to be granted the status as a poor household, and for these purposes must—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">complete and sign the prescribed forms; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">provide any other documentation as may be required by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__term_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__list_1__item_ii__term_1">municipality</span>;</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-applicant" id="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">applicant</span> may not be the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_2">owner</span> of more than one <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_3" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_3">property</span> and he or she must occupy the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_4" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_4">property</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">the collective household income may not exceed the amount determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1">municipality</span> in terms of subsection (2).</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_15__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">For the purposes of determining the collective household income as contemplated in subsection (1)(d), the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">municipality</span> may stipulate an amount, or may determine a maximum amount based on any one or more of the following:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">consumption of water;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">consumption of electricity; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the municipal valuation of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1">property</span>, which valuation may not exceed the value determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_2">municipality</span>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_15__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_15__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">In the case of a tenant—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_15__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the tenant must apply in <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_15__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1">person</span> and may qualify for electricity, water and refuse and sewage charges only, for which charges he or she must receive a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_account" id="sec_15__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_2">municipal account</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_15__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_15__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1">person</span> receiving the rent payable by the tenant whether on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_15__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_2">person</span>’s own account or as agent for any other <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_15__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_3" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_3">person</span> entitled thereto or interested therein, is responsible for rates.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_15__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">In the instance where the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_15__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_4__term_1">account holder</span> is deceased, the existing and future accounts of the household must be accepted under the indigence relief measures, on condition that only the surviving spouse or dependent children may apply or benefit.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_15__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The onus is on the head of an indigent household to notify the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_15__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_15__subsec_5__term_1">municipality</span> of any change in the circumstances which causes non-compliance with this section and at the same time furnish all detail with regard to such changed circumstances.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_16" data-eId="sec_16"><h3>16. Credit given</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_16__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_16__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Households which qualify for indigence relief measures may receive a credit for some or all of the following as determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_16__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">municipality</span>:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_16__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">a quantity of electricity plus basic fee;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_16__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">a quantity of water plus basic fee;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_16__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">refuse removal charges;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_16__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">sewerage charges;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_16__subsec_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">rates; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_16__subsec_1__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_1__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">any other service fees, taxes or charges over and above the rendered services.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_16__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_16__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_2__term_1">municipality</span> has the right to review an application for indigence relief on a regular basis and to visit the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_16__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_2__term_2">property</span> mentioned in section 15(1)(c) at any reasonable time for the purposes of verifying the information given in an application.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_16__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The normal rates, fees and charges and the requirement to pay an account will apply should a household account exceed the credit limits approved by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_16__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_3__term_1">municipality</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_16__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where it has been established that indigence relief has been granted on the basis of false or fraudulent information supplied, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_16__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_16__subsec_4__term_1">municipality</span> may withdraw such relief with immediate effect.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_17" data-eId="sec_17"><h3>17. Cancellation of registration</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_17__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Registration as an indigent household shall be cancelled in the cases mentioned below and such household shall forfeit all assistance granted for the unexpired term for which assistance was granted:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">where it is found that false information was furnished in the application or other documentation or statements;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">where the head of the indigent household refuses or fails to furnish the information required in terms of section 15(1)(b) for a period of 30 days after suspension of assistance because of failure to prove qualification for assistance;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_17__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">if it is found that circumstances have changed to such an extent that the indigent household no longer satisfies one or more of the requirements for registration.</span></span></span></span></section></section></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_3" data-eId="chp_3"><h2>Chapter 3<br>Tariffs</h2>
<section class="akn-part" id="chp_3__part_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_1"><h2>Part 1 – General principles, calculation of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-tariffs_for_major_services" id="chp_3__part_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_1__term_1">tariffs for major services</span>
</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_18" data-eId="sec_18"><h3>18. General principles</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_18__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_18__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_1__term_1">municipality</span> adopts, subject to subsection (14), sections 21(3)(d) and (e) and 22(5)(d), a two-part tariff structure consisting of a basic charge coupled with a charge based on consumption which tariffs may be adjusted during the financial year when such adjustment is required or approved in terms of national or provincial legislation.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_18__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_18__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">In setting its annual tariffs the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_18__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">municipality</span> must at all times take due cognisance of the—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_18__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">tariffs applicable elsewhere in the economic region; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_18__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">impact which its own tariffs may have on local economic development.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_18__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">With the exception of the indigence relief measures approved by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_18__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_3__term_1">municipality</span>, service tariffs imposed by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_18__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_3__term_2">municipality</span> should be viewed as user charges and not as taxes, and the ability of the relevant <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_18__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_3__term_3">consumer</span> or user of the services to which such tariffs relate, to pay for such services, should not be considered as a relevant criterion.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_18__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_18__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_4__term_1">municipality</span> must ensure that its tariffs are uniformly and fairly applied throughout the municipal area.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_18__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_18__subsec_5__list_1" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_5__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Tariffs for the following services rendered by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_18__subsec_5__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_5__list_1__term_1">municipality</span>, must as far as possible recover the expenses associated with the rendering of each service concerned, and, where feasible, generate a surplus as determined in each <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-annual_budget" id="sec_18__subsec_5__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_5__list_1__term_2">annual budget</span>:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_18__subsec_5__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_5__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">supply of electricity;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_18__subsec_5__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_5__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">supply of water;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_18__subsec_5__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_5__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">sanitation services, including sewerage and waste water disposal services;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_18__subsec_5__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_5__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">refuse (solids waste) removal services; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_18__subsec_5__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_5__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">any other services rendered by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_18__subsec_5__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_5__list_1__item_e__term_1">municipality</span>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_18__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The tariff, which a particular <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_18__subsec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_6__term_1">consumer</span> or user pays, must be directly related to the standard of service received and the quantity of the particular service used or consumed.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_18__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_18__subsec_7__list_1" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_7__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_18__subsec_7__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_7__list_1__term_1">municipality</span> must annually review its indigence relief measures, as contemplated in sections 15 and 16, and must set out the—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_18__subsec_7__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_7__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p"><span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_18__subsec_7__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_7__list_1__item_a__term_1">municipality</span>’s cost recovery policy in respect of the tariffs which it levies on registered indigents; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_18__subsec_7__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_7__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the implications of such policy for the tariffs which it imposes on other users and consumers in the municipal region.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_18__subsec_8" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_8"><span class="akn-num">(8)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_18__subsec_8__list_1" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_8__list_1"><span class="akn-item" id="sec_18__subsec_8__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_8__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_18__subsec_8__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_8__list_1__item_a__term_1">municipality</span>’s tariff policy must be transparent.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_18__subsec_8__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_8__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">The extent to which there is cross-subsidisation between categories of consumers or users must be evident to all consumers or users of the service in question.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_18__subsec_9" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_9"><span class="akn-num">(9)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_18__subsec_9__list_1" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_9__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_18__subsec_9__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_9__list_1__term_1">municipality</span> undertakes to—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_18__subsec_9__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_9__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">ensure that its tariffs are explained to and understood by all consumers and users affected by this by-law;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_18__subsec_9__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_9__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">render its services cost effectively in order to ensure the best possible cost of service delivery.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_18__subsec_10" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_10"><span class="akn-num">(10)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">In the case of the directly measurable services, namely electricity and water, the consumption of such services must be properly metered by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_18__subsec_10__term_1" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_10__term_1">municipality</span>, and meters must be read, wherever circumstances reasonably permit, on a monthly basis, and the charges levied on consumers must be proportionate to the quantity of the service which they consume.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_18__subsec_11" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_11"><span class="akn-num">(11)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">In considering the costing of its water, electricity and sewerage services, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_18__subsec_11__term_1" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_11__term_1">municipality</span> must take due cognisance of the high capital cost of establishing and expanding such services, and of the resultant high fixed costs, as opposed to variable costs of operating these services.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_18__subsec_12" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_12"><span class="akn-num">(12)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_18__subsec_12__list_1" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_12__list_1"><span class="akn-item" id="sec_18__subsec_12__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_12__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_18__subsec_12__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_12__list_1__item_a__term_1">municipality</span>’s tariffs for electricity services are determined to ensure that those consumers who are mainly responsible for peak demand, and therefor for the incurring by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_18__subsec_12__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_12__list_1__item_a__term_2">municipality</span> of the associated demand charges from Eskom, have to bear the costs associated with these charges.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_18__subsec_12__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_12__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">For the purposes of paragraph (a), the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_18__subsec_12__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_12__list_1__item_b__term_1">municipality</span> may install demand meters to measure the maximum demand of such consumers during certain periods.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_18__subsec_12__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_18__subsec_12__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">Such consumers must pay the relevant demand charge as well as a service charge directly related to their actual consumption of electricity during the relevant metering period.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_19" data-eId="sec_19"><h3>19. Calculation of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-tariffs_for_major_services" id="sec_19__term_1" data-eId="sec_19__term_1">tariffs for major services</span>
</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_19__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_19__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_19__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_19__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">In order to calculate the tariffs which must be charged for the supply of the services contemplated in section 18(5), the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_19__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_19__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1">municipality</span> must identify all the costs of operation of the undertakings concerned, including specifically the following:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_19__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_19__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">cost of bulk purchases in the case of water and electricity;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_19__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_19__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">distribution costs;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_19__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_19__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">distribution losses in the case of electricity and water;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_19__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_19__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">depreciation expenses;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_19__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_19__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">maintenance of infrastructure and other fixed assets;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_19__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_19__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_19__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__list_1" data-eId="sec_19__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">administration and service costs, including—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_19__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_19__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">service charges levied by other departments such as finance, human resources and legal services;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_19__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_19__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">reasonable general overheads, such as the costs associated with the office of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_manager" id="sec_19__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_ii__term_1" data-eId="sec_19__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_ii__term_1">municipal manager</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_19__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_19__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">adequate contributions to the provisions for bad debts and obsolescence of stock; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_19__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="sec_19__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">all other ordinary operating expenses associated with the service concerned including, in the case of the electricity service, the cost of providing street lighting in the municipal area; and</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_19__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_19__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">the cost of indigence relief measures.</span></span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-part" id="chp_3__part_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_2"><h2>Part 2 – Structure of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-tariffs_for_major_services" id="chp_3__part_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_3__part_2__term_1">tariffs for major services</span>, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-minor_tariffs" id="chp_3__part_2__term_2" data-eId="chp_3__part_2__term_2">minor tariffs</span>
</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_20" data-eId="sec_20"><h3>20. Structure of tariffs</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_20__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_20__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_20__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">municipality</span> may—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_20__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">determine the kilowatt-hours of electricity per <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-month" id="sec_20__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">month</span> and the kilolitres of water which will be provided free of charge to any category of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_20__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_1__list_1__item_a__term_2">consumer</span>;
