and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_20__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">consider relief in respect of the tariffs for sewerage and refuse removal for such registered indigent to the extent that the council deems such relief affordable in terms of each <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-annual_budget" id="sec_20__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">annual budget</span>, however, such relief may not be less than a discount as determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_20__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_1__list_1__item_b__term_2">municipality</span>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_20__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The tariff for consumption for a pre-paid meter is the same as the ordinary consumption tariffs levied on the category of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_20__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_2__term_1">consumer</span> concerned, and no basic charge is payable on a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_20__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_2__term_2">property</span> where a pre-paid meter has been installed.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_21" data-eId="sec_21"><h3>21. Electricity</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_21__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The various categories of electricity consumers, as set out in subsection (3), are charged at the applicable tariffs, as approved by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_21__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__term_1">municipality</span> in each <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-annual_budget" id="sec_21__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__term_2">annual budget</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_21__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Subject to section 18(1), tariff adjustments are effective in respect of July accounts each year.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_21__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_21__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Categories of consumers and charges are as follows:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_21__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">with the exception of a registered indigent, a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_21__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1">consumer</span> must be billed for all the electricity consumed at the tariff applicable to the category in which the particular <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_21__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_2">consumer</span> falls.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_21__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the tariff for domestic consumption of electricity may not exceed such percentage, per kilowatt-hours, as determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_21__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1">municipality</span>, of the tariff applicable to other consumers, and all consumers with the same type of connection must pay the same tariff per kilowatt-hour.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_21__subsec_3__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_3__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">electricity consumers of a category determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_21__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_1">municipality</span> must receive free the amount of kilowatt-hours of electricity as determined in terms of section 20(1).</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_21__subsec_3__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_3__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">a domestic electricity <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_21__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__term_1">consumer</span> other than a registered indigent and sub-economic (Government subsidised Housing) <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_21__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__term_2" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__term_2">consumer</span> may additionally be billed a basic charge per meter installed.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_21__subsec_3__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_3__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">a commercial, industrial and other non-domestic <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_21__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__term_1">property</span> may additionally be billed a monthly basic charge per meter installed and, where applicable, a demand charge appropriate to its respective levels of consumption.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_22" data-eId="sec_22"><h3>22. Water</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_22__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The categories of water consumers as set out in subsection (5), are charged at the applicable tariffs, as approved by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_22__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_1__term_1">municipality</span> in each <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-annual_budget" id="sec_22__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_1__term_2">annual budget</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_22__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Subject to section 18(1), tariff adjustments are effective in respect of July accounts each year.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_22__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The tariff levied for domestic consumption of water escalates according to the volume of water consumed, and will be based on a monthly consumption as determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_22__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_3__term_1">municipality</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_22__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The tariff for non-domestic water consumption is based on monthly consumption as determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_22__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_4__term_1">municipality</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_22__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_22__subsec_5__list_1" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_5__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Categories of consumers and charges are as follows:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_22__subsec_5__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_5__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">a domestic water <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_22__subsec_5__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_5__list_1__item_a__term_1">consumer</span> registered as an indigent with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_22__subsec_5__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_5__list_1__item_a__term_2">municipality</span> must receive free the first six kilolitre of water consumed per <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-month" id="sec_22__subsec_5__list_1__item_a__term_3" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_5__list_1__item_a__term_3">month</span>, thereafter a tariff as determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_22__subsec_5__list_1__item_a__term_4" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_5__list_1__item_a__term_4">municipality</span> is applicable on metered water consumption.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_22__subsec_5__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_5__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">all other domestic consumers are charged for actual water consumption at a stepped tariff per kilolitre as determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_22__subsec_5__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_5__list_1__item_b__term_1">municipality</span>.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_22__subsec_5__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_5__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the tariff applicable to domestic consumption of water may not exceed such percentage per kilolitre as determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_22__subsec_5__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_5__list_1__item_c__term_1">municipality</span>, of the tariff applicable to other consumers and all other consumers, including businesses, industries and institutional consumers, must pay the tariff as contemplated in subsection (4).</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_22__subsec_5__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_5__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">a basic charge per water meter, as determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_22__subsec_5__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_5__list_1__item_d__term_1">municipality</span>, is charged on a water <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer" id="sec_22__subsec_5__list_1__item_d__term_2" data-eId="sec_22__subsec_5__list_1__item_d__term_2">consumer</span>.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_23" data-eId="sec_23"><h3>23. Refuse removal</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_23__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The categories of refuse removal users as set out in subsection (3) are charged at the applicable tariffs, as approved by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_23__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_1__term_1">municipality</span> in each <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-annual_budget" id="sec_23__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_1__term_2">annual budget</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_23__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Subject to section 18(1), tariff adjustments are effective in respect of July accounts each year.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_23__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_23__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A separate fixed monthly refuse removal charge applies to each of the following categories of users, based on the costs of the service concerned:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_3__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_3__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">domestic and other users, where refuse is removed by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_23__subsec_3__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_3__list_1__item_i__term_1">municipality</span> once weekly; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_3__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_3__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">business and other users, where refuse is removed by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_23__subsec_3__list_1__item_ii__term_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_3__list_1__item_ii__term_1">municipality</span> twice weekly;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_3__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_3__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">business and other users, where refuse is removed by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_23__subsec_3__list_1__item_iii__term_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_3__list_1__item_iii__term_1">municipality</span> thrice weekly; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_23__subsec_3__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_3__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">business and other bulk consumers.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_23__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A registered indigent may receive a discount on this charge as the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_23__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_4__term_1">municipality</span> deems affordable when approving each <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-annual_budget" id="sec_23__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_4__term_2">annual budget</span>, which discount may not be less than the percentage, as determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_23__subsec_4__term_3" data-eId="sec_23__subsec_4__term_3">municipality</span>, of the monthly amount billed as a refuse removal charge.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_24" data-eId="sec_24"><h3>24. Sewerage</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_24__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The categories of sewerage users as set out in subsection (3) are charged per <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-month" id="sec_24__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1__term_1">month</span> at the applicable tariff as approved by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_24__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1__term_2">municipality</span> in each <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-annual_budget" id="sec_24__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_1__term_3">annual budget</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_24__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Subject to section 18(1), tariff adjustments are effective in respect of July accounts each year.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_24__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_24__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Categories of users and charges are:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_24__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-availability_charge" id="sec_24__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1">availability charge</span> is charged per <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-month" id="sec_24__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_2">month</span> or annually for an undeveloped erf, irrespective of its permitted or intended use.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_24__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">a fixed monthly charge based on the costs of the service, is charged for a domestic user, however, a registered indigent may receive such discount on this charge as the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_24__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1">municipality</span> deems affordable when approving each <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-annual_budget" id="sec_24__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_2">annual budget</span>, which discount may not be less than the percentage, as determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_24__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_3" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_3">municipality</span>, of the monthly amount billed for this service.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_24__subsec_3__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_3__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">a fixed monthly charge based on the costs of the service is charged for a domestic user, however, a registered indigent may receive such discount on this charge as the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_24__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_1">municipality</span> deems affordable when approving each <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-annual_budget" id="sec_24__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_2">annual budget</span>, which discount may not be less than the percentage, as determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_24__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_3" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_3">municipality</span>, of the monthly amount billed for this service.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_24__subsec_3__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_3__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">a fixed monthly charge based on the costs of the service is charged to all businesses, industries and institutional users.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_24__subsec_3__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_3__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">an effluent fee is payable by a factory and another industrial user where the wastewater emanating from such user requires special purification measures by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_24__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__term_1">municipality</span>, and the fee is based on the toxic content of the wastewater concerned and the costs of the purification.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_24__subsec_3__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_3__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">a tariff, at a cost determined annually in the budget, will be levied for each visit to empty a septic tank on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_24__subsec_3__list_1__item_f__term_1" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_3__list_1__item_f__term_1">premises</span> of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_24__subsec_3__list_1__item_f__term_2" data-eId="sec_24__subsec_3__list_1__item_f__term_2">person</span> requiring such service.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_25" data-eId="sec_25"><h3>25. Minor tariffs</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_25__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">All <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-minor_tariffs" id="sec_25__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_1__term_1">minor tariffs</span> are standardised within the municipal region.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_25__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_25__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">All <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-minor_tariffs" id="sec_25__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">minor tariffs</span> are approved by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_25__subsec_2__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_2__list_1__term_2">municipality</span> in each <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-annual_budget" id="sec_25__subsec_2__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_2__list_1__term_3">annual budget</span> and are, when deemed appropriate by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_25__subsec_2__list_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_2__list_1__term_4">municipality</span>, subsidised by <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_25__subsec_2__list_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_2__list_1__term_5">property</span> rates and general revenues, particularly when the—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_25__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">tariffs prove uneconomical when charged to cover the cost of the service concerned;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_25__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">cost cannot accurately be determined; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_25__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">tariff is designed purely to regulate rather than finance the use of the particular service or amenity.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_25__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Unless there are compelling reasons why such adjustment should not be effected, all <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-minor_tariffs" id="sec_25__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_3__term_1">minor tariffs</span> over which the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_25__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_3__term_2">municipality</span> has full control, and which are not directly related to the cost of a particular service, are adjusted annually at least in accordance with the prevailing <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-consumer_price_index" id="sec_25__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_3__term_3">consumer price index</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_25__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_25__subsec_4__list_1" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_4__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The following services are subsidised services, and the tariffs levied cover 50%, or as near as possible to 50%, of the annual operating expenses budgeted for the service concerned:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_25__subsec_4__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_4__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">burial services and the provision of cemeteries; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_25__subsec_4__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_4__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the provision of municipal sports facilities for use against a fee.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_25__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_25__subsec_5__list_1" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_5__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The following services are considered as being community services, and no tariffs are levied for their use:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_25__subsec_5__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_5__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">a municipal swimming pool;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_25__subsec_5__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_5__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">a municipal museum and art gallery;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_25__subsec_5__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_5__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the disposal of garden refuse at the municipal disposal site;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_25__subsec_5__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_5__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">a municipal reference library;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_25__subsec_5__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_5__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">a municipal lending library, except for fines determined;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_25__subsec_5__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_5__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">a municipal botanical garden, other park or open space;</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_25__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_25__subsec_6__list_1" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_6__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The following services are considered as being economic services, and the tariffs levied cover 100%, or as near as possible to 100%, of the budgeted annual operating expenses of the service concerned:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_25__subsec_6__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_6__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">The maintenance of graves, gardens of remembrance and crematoria against payment of a fee;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_25__subsec_6__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_6__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the availability of a house against payment of a housing rental;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_25__subsec_6__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_6__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">subject to subsection (9), the use of a municipal hall and other <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_25__subsec_6__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_6__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">the supply of a building plan against payment of a fee;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_25__subsec_6__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_6__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_25__subsec_6__list_1__item_e__list_1" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_6__list_1__item_e__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">the selling of—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_25__subsec_6__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_6__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">plastic refuse bags;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_25__subsec_6__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_6__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">the selling of refuse bins; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_25__subsec_6__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_6__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">livestock and plants;</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" fee;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_25__subsec_6__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_6__list_1__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">the connection of electricity, water and sewerage against payment of a connection fee;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_25__subsec_6__list_1__item_h" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_6__list_1__item_h"><span data-eId="sec_25__subsec_6__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">the issuing of a clearance certificate against payment of a fee.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_25__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_25__subsec_7__list_1" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_7__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The following charges and tariffs are considered as regulatory or punitive, and are determined as appropriate in each <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-annual_budget" id="sec_25__subsec_7__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_7__list_1__term_1">annual budget</span>:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_25__subsec_7__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_7__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">fines for lost or overdue library books;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_25__subsec_7__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_7__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">advertising sign fees;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_25__subsec_7__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_7__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">pound fees;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_25__subsec_7__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_7__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">disconnection and reconnection fees of electricity and water;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_25__subsec_7__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_7__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">penalty and other charges imposed in terms of Chapters 1 and 2; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_25__subsec_7__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_7__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">penalty charges for the submission of dishonoured, stale, post-dated or otherwise unacceptable cheques.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_25__subsec_8" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_8"><span class="akn-num">(8)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The costs of the democratic process in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_25__subsec_8__term_1" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_8__term_1">municipality</span> such as, but not limited to, all expenses associated with the political structures of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_25__subsec_8__term_2" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_8__term_2">municipality</span>, form part of the expenses to be financed from <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_25__subsec_8__term_3" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_8__term_3">property</span> rates and general revenues, and are not included in the costing of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-major_services" id="sec_25__subsec_8__term_4" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_8__term_4">major services</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_25__subsec_8__term_5" data-eId="sec_25__subsec_8__term_5">municipality</span>.</span></span></section></section></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_4" data-eId="chp_4"><h2>Chapter 4<br>Availability charges</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_26" data-eId="sec_26"><h3>26. Availability charges</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_26__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_26__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Availability charges in respect of water, electricity, sewerage and refuse removal, as determined annually in the budget by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_26__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_26__hcontainer_1__term_1">municipality</span>, is payable by all owners of undeveloped <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_26__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_26__hcontainer_1__term_2">property</span> where none of the said services are connected, but can be reasonably connected. If one or more of the services are connected, then the basic charge in respect of all the services that can reasonably be connected shall still apply.</span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_5" data-eId="chp_5"><h2>Chapter 5<br>Enforcement</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_27" data-eId="sec_27"><h3>27. Municipality’s powers to restrict or disconnect supply of services</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1">municipality</span> may, over and above the provisions of any other provisions in this by-law restrict or disconnect the supply of water and electricity, or discontinue any other service to any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_2">premises</span> if—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">an administration order is granted in terms of section 74 of the Magistrates Court Act, 1944 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1944/37" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1944/37">Act 37 of 1944</a>), in respect of an account holder; provided further that such services will only be suspended if the account holder fails to make regular payments in respect of the current services;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">account holder</span> of any service fails to comply with a condition of supply imposed by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_2">municipality</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">account holder</span> obstructs the efficient supply of electricity, water or any other municipal services to another <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__term_2">account holder</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_1">account holder</span> supplies such municipal services to any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_2" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_2">person</span> who is not entitled thereto or permits such service to continue;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e__term_1">account holder</span> causes a situation which is dangerous or a contravention of relevant legislation; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__term_1" data-eId="sec_27__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__term_1">account holder</span> is placed under provisional registration, liquidation or judicial management, or commits an act of insolvency in terms of the Insolvency Act, 1936 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1936/24" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1936/24">Act 24 of 1936</a>).</span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_28" data-eId="sec_28"><h3>28. Tampering, unauthorised connections and reconnections, and improper use</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_28__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_28__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_1__term_1">municipality</span> reserves the right to monitor the service network for signs of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-tampering" id="sec_28__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_1__term_2">tampering</span> or irregularities.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_28__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_28__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_2__term_1">person</span> may in any manner or for any reason tamper or interfere with any meter or metering equipment or service connection or service protective device or supply mains or any other equipment of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_28__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_2__term_2">municipality</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_28__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where evidence exists of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_28__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_3__term_1">account holder</span> or any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_28__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_3__term_2">person</span> having contravened subsection (2), the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_28__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_3__term_3">municipality</span> has the right to disconnect the supply immediately and without prior notice to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_28__subsec_3__term_4" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_3__term_4">account holder</span>, and the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_28__subsec_3__term_5" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_3__term_5">account holder</span> is liable for all fees and charges levied by the Municipality for such disconnection.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_28__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_28__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_4__term_1">account holder</span> or any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_28__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_4__term_2">person</span> has contravened subsection (2) and such contravention has resulted in the meter recording less than the true consumption, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_28__subsec_4__term_3" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_4__term_3">municipality</span> has the right to recover from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_28__subsec_4__term_4" data-eId="sec_28__subsec_4__term_4">account holder</span> the full cost of his or her estimated consumption.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_29" data-eId="sec_29"><h3>29. Clearance certificate</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_29__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_29__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">To effect the transfer of any immovable <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_29__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_29__hcontainer_1__term_1">property</span> from one registered <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_29__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_29__hcontainer_1__term_2">owner</span> to another, the Registrar of Deeds requires a clearance certificate, which certificate is obtainable from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_manager" id="sec_29__hcontainer_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_29__hcontainer_1__term_3">municipal manager</span> upon payment of the prescribed fee and subject to the conditions of section 118 of the Municipal Systems Act, 2000 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/2000/32" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/2000/32">Act 32 of 2000</a>) being met.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_30" data-eId="sec_30"><h3>30. Tenders and grants-in-aid</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_30__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Each tender submitted to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_30__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1__term_1">municipality</span> must be accompanied by a certificate from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_30__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1__term_2">municipality</span> stating that the proposed supplier/service provider is not indebted to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_30__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1__term_3">municipality</span> for any arrear amount reflected on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_account" id="sec_30__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_1__term_4">municipal account</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_30__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Should a proposed supplier or service provider be so indebted, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_30__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_2__term_1">municipality</span> may disallow the tender.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_30__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_30__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_3__term_1">municipality</span> may only consider a tender once the proposed supplier or service provider has made satisfactory arrangements to pay the outstanding amount by means of instalments, or has settled all arrear amounts in full.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_30__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_manager" id="sec_30__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_4__term_1">municipal manager</span> or a duly authorised <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-officer" id="sec_30__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_4__term_2">officer</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_30__subsec_4__term_3" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_4__term_3">municipality</span> must in the condition of contract, provide for the deduction from moneys owed to the supplier or service provider in order to settle any outstanding amount.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_30__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Payment of any grants-in-aid approved by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_30__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_5__term_1">municipality</span> may be withheld pending payment of any outstanding <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_account" id="sec_30__subsec_5__term_2" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_5__term_2">municipal account</span>, or pending an agreement between the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_30__subsec_5__term_3" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_5__term_3">municipality</span> and the receiver of a grant-in-aid in which satisfactory arrangements have been made regarding the settlement of the outstanding <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_account" id="sec_30__subsec_5__term_4" data-eId="sec_30__subsec_5__term_4">municipal account</span>.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_31" data-eId="sec_31"><h3>31. Power of council to recover costs</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_31__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where a bank dishonours any payment made to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_31__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_1__term_1">municipality</span>, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_31__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_1__term_2">municipality</span> may levy and recover all related costs and any administration fees against an account of the defaulting <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_31__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_1__term_3">account holder</span> and may disconnect or restrict the supplies to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_31__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_1__term_4">premises</span> of such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_31__subsec_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_1__term_5">account holder</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_31__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">All legal costs, excluding attorney-and-client costs incurred in the recovery of amounts in arrears and payable in terms of the Magistrates Court Act, 1944 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1944/32" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1944/32">Act 32 of 1944</a>), must be levied against the arrears account of the account holder.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_31__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">For any action taken in demanding payment from an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_31__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_3__term_1">account holder</span> or reminding an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_31__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_3__term_2">account holder</span> by means of telephone, fax, electronic mail, letter or otherwise that payments are due, a fee will be levied against the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_account" id="sec_31__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_3__term_3">municipal account</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_31__subsec_3__term_4" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_3__term_4">account holder</span> in terms of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_31__subsec_3__term_5" data-eId="sec_31__subsec_3__term_5">municipality</span>’s tariff policy.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_32" data-eId="sec_32"><h3>32. Prima facie evidence</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_32__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_32__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Acertificate reflecting the amount due and payable to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_32__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_32__hcontainer_1__term_1">municipality</span>, signed by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_manager" id="sec_32__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_32__hcontainer_1__term_2">municipal manager</span>, is upon mere production thereof prima facie evidence of the indebtedness of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_32__hcontainer_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_32__hcontainer_1__term_3">person</span> mentioned in it.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_33" data-eId="sec_33"><h3>33. Abandonment of bad debts, and full and final settlement of account</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_33__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Before terminating the debt collection procedure in any individual instance, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_manager" id="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">municipal manager</span> must—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">ensure that all debt collection mechanisms as provided for in section 11 have been utilised where reasonable;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">maintain an audit trail; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">document the reasons for terminating the debt collection procedure, including the cost of enforcement and necessary financial adjustments.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_33__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_manager" id="sec_33__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_2__term_1">municipal manager</span> may consider an offer for full and final settlement, and must, if in the interests of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_33__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_2__term_2">municipality</span>, in writing consent to the acceptance of a lesser amount as full and final settlement of the amount due and payable.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_33__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where the exact amount due and payable to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_33__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_3__term_1">municipality</span> has not been paid in full, any lesser amount tendered to and accepted by any municipal employee, except the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_manager" id="sec_33__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_33__subsec_3__term_2">municipal manager</span>, shall not be deemed to be in full and final settlement of such an amount.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_34" data-eId="sec_34"><h3>34. Power of entry and inspection</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_34__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A duly authorised representative of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_34__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_1__term_1">municipality</span> may for any reason related to the implementation or enforcement of this by-law at all reasonable times or in emergency at any time, enter <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_34__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_1__term_2">premises</span>, request information and carry out such inspection as deemed necessary, and may for purposes of installing or repairing any meter or service connection for reticulation disconnect, stop or restrict the provision of any service.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_34__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_34__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">If the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_34__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">municipality</span> considers it necessary for work to be performed to enable an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-officer" id="sec_34__subsec_2__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_2__list_1__term_2">officer</span> to perform a function referred to in subsection (1) properly and effectively, it may—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_34__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">by written notice require an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_34__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">account holder</span> to do, at own expense, specified work within a specified period; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_34__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">if the situation is a matter of urgency, without prior notice do such work or cause it to be done at the expense of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_34__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">account holder</span>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_34__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If the work referred to in subsection (2) is carried out for the sole purpose of establishing whether a contravention of this by-law has been committed and no such contravention has taken place, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_34__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_3__term_1">municipality</span> must bear the expense connected therewith together with that of restoring the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_34__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_34__subsec_3__term_2">premises</span> to their former condition.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_35" data-eId="sec_35"><h3>35. Authentication and service of orders, notices and other documents</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_35__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An order, notice or other document requiring authentication by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_35__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__term_1">municipality</span> must be signed by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_manager" id="sec_35__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__term_2">municipal manager</span> and when issued by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_35__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__term_3">municipality</span> in terms of this by-law is deemed to be duly issued if it is signed by an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-officer" id="sec_35__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__term_4">officer</span> authorised by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_35__subsec_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_1__term_5">municipality</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_35__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Any notice or other document that is served on a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">person</span> by a duly authorised <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-officer" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__term_2">officer</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__term_3">municipality</span> in terms of this by-law, is regarded as having been served—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">when it has been delivered to that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">person</span> personally;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">when it has been left at that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">person</span>’s place of residence or business in the Republic with a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_2">person</span> apparently over the age of 16 years;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">when it has been posted by registered or certified mail to that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1">person</span>’s last known residential or business address in the Republic and an acknowledgement of the posting thereof from the postal service is obtained;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">if that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_1">person</span>’s address in the Republic is unknown, when it has been served on that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_2" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_2">person</span>’s agent or representative in the Republic in the manner provided by paragraphs (a), (b) or (c);</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">if that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_e__term_1">person</span>’s address and agent or representative in the Republic is unknown, when it has been placed in a conspicuous place on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_e__term_2" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_e__term_2">property</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_e__term_3" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_e__term_3">premises</span>, if any, to which it relates;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">in the event of a body corporate, when it has been delivered at the registered office of the business <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-premises" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__term_1" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__term_1">premises</span> of such body corporate to a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__term_2" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__term_2">person</span> apparently over the age of 16 years; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">when it has been delivered, at the request of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_g__term_1" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_g__term_1">person</span>, to that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_g__term_2" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_2__list_1__item_g__term_2">person</span>’s electronic mail address.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_35__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">When any notice or other document has to be served on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_35__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_3__term_1">owner</span>, an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_35__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_3__term_2">account holder</span> or holder of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_35__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_3__term_3">property</span> or right in any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_35__subsec_3__term_4" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_3__term_4">property</span>, it is sufficient if that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_35__subsec_3__term_5" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_3__term_5">person</span> is described in the notice or other document as the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-owner" id="sec_35__subsec_3__term_6" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_3__term_6">owner</span>, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-account_holder" id="sec_35__subsec_3__term_7" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_3__term_7">account holder</span> or holder of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-property" id="sec_35__subsec_3__term_8" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_3__term_8">property</span> or right in question, and it is not necessary to name that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_35__subsec_3__term_9" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_3__term_9">person</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_35__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Service of a copy is deemed to be service of the original.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_35__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any legal process is effectively and sufficiently served on the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_35__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_5__term_1">municipality</span> when it is delivered to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_manager" id="sec_35__subsec_5__term_2" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_5__term_2">municipal manager</span> or a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_35__subsec_5__term_3" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_5__term_3">person</span> in attendance at the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipal_manager" id="sec_35__subsec_5__term_4" data-eId="sec_35__subsec_5__term_4">municipal manager</span>’s office.</span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_6" data-eId="chp_6"><h2>Chapter 6<br>General provisions</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_36" data-eId="sec_36"><h3>36. Right of appeal</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_36__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_36__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_36__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_36__hcontainer_1__term_1">person</span> whose rights are affected by a decision of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_36__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_36__hcontainer_1__term_2">municipality</span> may appeal against that decision by giving written notice of the appeal and the reasons therefor in terms of section 62 of the Local Government: Municipal Systems Act, <a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/2000/32" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/2000/32">Act 32 of 2000</a> to the municipal manager within 21 days of the date of the notification of the decision</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_37" data-eId="sec_37"><h3>37. Offences and penalties</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_37__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_37__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1">person</span> is, on conviction, and subject to penalties prescribed in any other law, liable to a fine or in default of payment, to imprisonment, or to such imprisonment without the option of a fine, or to both such fine and such imprisonment, and in the case of a successive or continuing offence, to a fine for every day such offence continues, or in default of payment thereof, to imprisonment if he or she—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">fails to give access required by an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-officer" id="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">officer</span> in terms of section 34;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">obstructs or hinders an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-officer" id="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">officer</span> in the exercise of his or her powers or the performance of functions or duties under this by-law;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">uses or interferes with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">municipality</span>’s equipment for consumption of services supplied;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">fails or refuses to give the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_1">municipality</span> or an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-officer" id="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_2" data-eId="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_2">officer</span> such information as the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_3" data-eId="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_3">municipality</span> or the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-officer" id="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_4" data-eId="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_4">officer</span> may reasonably require for the purpose of exercising powers or functions under this by-law, or gives the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_5" data-eId="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_5">municipality</span> or the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-officer" id="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_6" data-eId="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__term_6">officer</span> false or misleading information knowing it to be false or misleading;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">fails to comply with the terms of a notice served upon him or her in terms of this by-law; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">tampers or breaks any seal on a meter or on any equipment belonging to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__term_1" data-eId="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__term_1">municipality</span>, or for any reason causes a meter not to register the services used properly, and the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__term_2" data-eId="sec_37__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_f__term_2">person</span> shall furthermore be charged for usage of electricity or water, as the case may be.</span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_38" data-eId="sec_38"><h3>38. Repeal of by-laws</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_38__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_38__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any by-law previously promulgated by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_38__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_38__hcontainer_1__term_1">municipality</span> or any of the disestablished municipalities now incorporated into the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_38__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_38__hcontainer_1__term_2">municipality</span>, in so far as it relates to any matter provided for in this by-law is hereby repealed</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_39" data-eId="sec_39"><h3>39. Conflict with other legislation</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_39__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_39__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">In the event of any conflict between any provision of this by-law and National and Provincial legislation, standards, policies or guidelines, the National and Provincial Legislation, standards, policies or guidelines shall prevail.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_40" data-eId="sec_40"><h3>40. Short title and commencement</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_40__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_40__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">This by-law may be cited as the Credit Control, Tariffs and Debt Collection By-law and commences on the date of publication thereof in the Provincial Gazette.</span></span></span></section></section></span></article></span>
